\bentry
\word[U(1)]{U}
\pron{yU}
\gl{\nA} (\bava\ \eng{Us} yA \eng{U's} )
\dictmeaning{(\eng{u} eMdU \parx) 
\num{1}iMgilxSf vaNRmAleya ipapxtotxMdaneya akaSxra.
\num{2} \eng{U} AkArada vasutx
yA vakarx(reVKe) (\kanmu\ \saMpa gaLalilx baLake): \eng{U-bolt.}}
\eentry

birudu.}

--illxda, --alalxda, --Agirada: \eng{unusable, uncalled-for, 
uneducated, unfailing, unofficially, unhappiness.}

\bentry
\word{understand} 
\pron{aMDarfsATxYxMDf}
\gl{\kirx} (\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{understood} \ucAcx-- aMDarfsuTxDf). 

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (mAtugaLu, vayxkitx, BASe, \mo vugaLa) athaR -- garxhisu,
hiDi; athaRmADiko; ari(tuko); tiLi(duko): \eng{does not
 understand what you say} niVnu heVLuvudu(avanige)
athaRvAguvudillx. \eng{understands you perfectly} ninanxnunx
pUNRvAgi aritukoMDidAdxne. \eng{cannot understand French}
pherxMcfBASeyanunx athaRmADikoLaLxlAra.
\num{2} (udedxVsha, vivaraNe yA
kAraNvanunx) garxhisu; ari; tiLi; Uhisu; gotutx mADiko; athaR mADiko:
\eng{do not understand why he came} avanu yAke baMdanoV nanage
tiLiyadu. \eng{could not understand what the noise was about} A
galATe yAvudara bagegx eMbaudu gotAtxgalillx. \eng{do not
 understand the point of his remark} avana TiVkeya aMshavanunx
nAnu athaRmADikoLaLxlAre.
\num{3} (yAvudAdarU sUcane yA mAhitiya
AdhArada meVle Uhe, tiVmARna, \mo vugaLige baruvalilx) naMbau; eNisu;
Uhisu; BAvisu; takiRsu: \eng{I understand that it begins at
 noon} adu madhAyxhanx pArxraMBavAgutatxdeMdu nananx Uhe. \eng{I
 understand that expenses were to be paid} KcuRmADiruvudanunx
tuMbikoDalAgutatxdeMdu nAnu eNisutetxVne.
\num{4} (AshacxyaR, koVpa,
saMdeVha, \mo vanunx sUcisuvAga) tiLi; garxhisu; aMduko: \eng{am I to
 understand that you refuse?} niVnu nirAkarisutitxVyeMdu
tiLiyaleV?
\num{5} (manasisxnalilx) (padavanunx) adhAyxhAra mADiko:
\eng{the verb may be either expressed or understood} kirxyApada
vAcayxvAgirabahudu yA adhAyxhAravAgirabahudu.
\num{6} lkaSxN yA
savxBAvavanunx sahAnuBUtiyiMda -- athaRmADiko, tiLi, gamanisu,
aritiru: \eng{quite understand your difficulty} ninanx kaSaTx
nanage athaRvAgutatxde (nAnu balelx). \eng{cannot understand him
 at all} avananunx athaRmADikoLuLxvudeV kaSaTx.
\num{7}(heVge nivaRhisabeVkeMbaudanunx, vayxvaharisabeVkeMbaudanunx) aritiru;
athaRmADikoMDiru: \eng{could never understand algebra}
biVjgaNitavanunx eMdU athaRmADikoLaLxlAgiradavanAgidedx.}}

\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (sAmAnayxvAgi yA vishiSaTx athaRdalilx) athaRvAgu; arivAgu.
\num{2} (UheyiMda yA Kcita AdhArada meVle) tiLi; garxhisu;
naMbau: \eng{he is coming to -- morrow, I understand} (avanu nALe
barutAtxneMdu keVLide, hwde?) avanu nALe barutitxdAdxneMdu
tiLididedxVne.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{give(1) pagu(16)}{${}^1$give} person to understand .}
\num{2} \eng{tongue not understanded of the people} (\pArxparx)
jnakekx athaRvAgadidadx paricayavillxdidadx BASe, anayxBASe, paraBASe.
\num{3} \eng{understand each other} 

\alnum{a} obabxrigobabxru
athaRmADikoLiLx; parasapxrara aBipArxya, BAvane, \mo vanunx
garxhisikoLiLx. 

\alnum{b} parasapxra omamxtadalilxri yA oLasaMcinalilx BAgigaLAgiri.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{undo} 
\pron{anfDU}
\gl{\akirx} (vataRmAnakAl \parxpu\ \Eva\ \eng{undoes}; \BU\ \eng{undid}; \BUkaq\ \eng{undone}).
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (aMgi, guMDi, BAMgi,
\mo vanunx) bicucx; tege; kaLacu: \eng{my shoelace has become
 undone} nananx pAdarakeSxya dAra bicicxhoVgide.
\num{2} (vayxkitxya
 baTeTx \mo vanunx) bicucx; kaLacu; tegeduhAku.
\num{3} radudxgoLisu; illxvAgisu; toDeduhAku: \eng{cannot undo the past} hiMde
 naDedadadxnunx toDeduhAkalu sAdhayxvillx.
\num{4} (hesaru, sananxDate, \mo vanunx) keDisu; hALu mADu; nAshakikxVDu mADu
 (\kanmu\ \BUkaq dalilx Iga \viparx): \eng{`alas! I am undone' she sobbed out} `ayoyxV! nAnu keTeTx' eMdu avaLu bikikxbikikx 
atatxLu.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word{unearth} 
\pron{anatfR}

bagegx hosa viSayagaLanunx beLakige taru.

\bentry

\pron{yUnayxnf, yUnianf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} okakxTuTx; okUkxT; aikayx; seVrike; saMyoVga: \eng{the union of the parts was imperfect} BAgagaLa seVrike 
asamapaRkavAgitutx.
\num{2} maduve; vivAha (saMbaMdha): \eng{a happy union} suKvAda vivAha saMbaMdha.
\num{3} hoMdike; sAmarasayx; sAMgatayx; meYtirx; EkiVBAva: \eng{lived together in perfect union} saMpUNRvAda meYtirxyiMda oMdAgi 
jiVvana naDesidaru.
\num{4} (vividha BAgagaLu seVri racitavAgiruva) rAjkiVya okUkxT: 

\alnum{a} (\kanmu) amerikada saMyukatx saMsAthxnagaLu. 

\alnum{b} gerxVTf birxTnf matutx \kanu\ aileRMDu. 

\alnum{c} dakiSxN Aphirxkada okUkxT. 

\alnum{d} soVviyeTf okUkxT.
\num{5} (\ga) kUT; eraDu athavA hecucx gaN \eng{(set)} gaLige seVrida ellx dhAtugaLanUnx oLagoMDa motatx.
\num{6} saMGa; saMGaTne; aMgaBAgagaLu yA sadasayxru parasapxra kUDi racitavAda okUkxTda vayxvasethx.
\num{7} 
\alnum{a} (\ca) pAyxriSf kUT; saMyukatx pAyxriSf; nigaRtikara jiVvanAdhAra kAnUnugaLa nivARhakAkxgi oMdugUDisida 
halvu pAyxriSfgaLu. 

\hypertarget{union(7)b}{}
\alnum{b} iMtha saMyukatx pAyxriSf sAthxpisida UT-vasati odagisuva, nigaRtikara Alya; anAthAlya.
\num{8} (\birx) (sahakArakAkxgi) oMdugUDisida cacuRgaLa kUT.
\num{9} \alnum{a} (vishavxvidAyxnilyada yA kAleVjina) vidAyxthiR saMGa yA cacARsaMGa: \eng{the debate at the Oxford union} 
AkfsxphaDfR vidAyxthiRsaMGadalilx naDeda cacARkUT. 

\alnum{b} iMtha saMGada vasati kaTTxDagaLu.
\num{10} gerxVTf birxTninxna dhavxjdalilx (rUDhiyAgi dhavxjsatxMBada
magugxlina meVlu mUleyalilx kANuva) okUkxT cihenx.  
\num{11} (koLave \mo vugaLanunx sulBavAgi kUDisalu yA beVpaRDisalu
baLasuva) joVDaNe salkaraNe; saMyoVjka.

    height 0.5cm {U_Pictures/union.jpg}}}
\num{12} (hatitx, linanf, reVSemx yA seNbau, \mo vugaLa) misharx neyegx baTeTx. 
\num{13} \alnum{a} ogUgxDike; saMyoVjne; saMGaTne; oMdugUDuvudu. 

\alnum{b} ogUgxDida sithxti; saMyukatx sithxti; saMGaTita sithxti. 
\num{14} vaqtitx saMGa; vaqtitxnirataru, kAmiRkaru tamamx aBivaqdithx matutx hitarakaSxNegAgi EpaRDisikoMDa okUkxT.}}

\pron{anfsAYxca(Tuyx)reVSanf} 
\gl{\nA} 
\dictmeaning{(\ravi) apayARpatxte: 

\alnum{a} (dArxvaNda \vi) inUnx hecucx dArxvayxvanunx viliVna
mADikoLaLxbalilxke.

\alnum{b} (kAbaRnika saMyukatxda \vi) racaneyalilx divxbaMdha yA
tirxbaMdhagaLiruva, AdadxriMdaleV saMkalna irxyegaLalilx 
pAlogxLaLxbalilxke.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[until(1)]{until} 
\pron{anfTilf} 
\gl{\upa} 
\dictmeaning{\num{1} (\kanmu\ vAkayx AraMBisuvAga, matutx aupacArika 
sheYliyalilx \parx) -varegU; -varege; -tanaka: \eng{until you told me I had no idea of it} niVnu heVLuvavaregU nanage adara kalpxneyeV iralillx.
\num{2} (niSeVdhAthaRka racaneyalilx): \eng{he did not go until night} 
rAtirxyavaregU avanu hoVgalillx.
\num{3} (vidhuyxkatxvAda baLakeyalilx): \eng{resided there until his death} 
avanu tiVrihoVguvavaregU alilx vAsavAgidadx. }

{\dictmeaning{(\pArxparx) \eng{= \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{to(1)}{${}^1$to}.}

inonxbabxra viSayadalilx oMdu riVtiyalilx naDeduko. \eng{sick (\engit{or}
faithful) unto death} koneya gaLigeyavaregU roVgagarxsatxnAgi (yA
niSeThxyiMda kUDi). }}

\eng{untouched lands} hokukx baLasada deVshagaLu.

\num{5} hAnige IDAgada.
\num{6} (yAvudariMdalU) parxBAvitavAgada; pariNAmagoLaLxda; mApARDAgada:

avaLa meVle yAva pariNAmavanUnx biVralillx.

\bentry
\word[up(1)]{up} 
\pron{apf} 
\gl{\kirxvi} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} meVle; meVlkekx; meVlugaDe (yalilx); meVlugaDege: \eng{high up in the air} (meVle) AkAshadalilx. \eng{what are they doing up there?} alilx meVle avaru Enu mADutitxdAdxre? \eng{lives four floors up} meVle nAlkxneya aMtasitxnalilx vAsisutAtxne. \eng{went up three places in class} avanu taragatiyalilx mUru sAthxna(daSuTx) meVlkekxVrida.
\num{2} (\AmA) alilx muMdugaDe; alilx meVlugaDe: \eng{went up front} muMdina sAlige hoVda.
\num{3} (hiMde) yAvudoV kAldavarege. 
\num{4} nadiya meVlkekx, mUldavarege: \eng{follow a stream up to its source} nadiya meVlkekx, mUldavarege (jADu hiDidu) hoVgu. 
\num{5} oLanADinalilx.
\num{6} (jUjukudureya savArana \vi) kudure Eri, hatitx.
\num{7} oMdu samathaR yA kAyARtamxkavAda yA parxgatiya sithxtiyalilx yA sithxtige: \eng{stirred up trouble} samaseyx huTuTx hAkida. \eng{the house is up for sale} mane mArATkikxde. \eng{the hunt is up} beVTe yA shoVdhane shuru Agide.
\num{8} kalitu yA tiLidu: \eng{is well up in French} pherxMcanunx cenAnxgi kalitukoMDidAdxne.
\num{9} (rasetx \mo vugaLa \vi) ripeVriyalilx; durasitxnalilx. 
\num{10} 
\alnum{a} (ATda gellxMka yA sokxVrina \vi) sokxVrf boVDiRnalilx dAKle mADi, noVMdaNisi; yAvudoV oMdu samayadalilx oTuTx motatxvAgi; oMdu taMDa yA obabx ATgArana inonxMdu taMDa yA ATgArana motatxkikxMta miVrisida motatxvAgi: \eng{our team is 3 goals up} namamx taMDa mUru goVlu gaLiside yA mUru goVlugaLiMda muMdide. 

\alnum{b} (ATgArana \vi) (hAge inonxMdu taMDa yA ATgAranigiMta) hecucx gellxMka gaLisi. 
\num{11} nAyxyAlya yA nAyxyAdhiVshana muMde hAjrupaDisi: \eng{was brought up for speeding} ati veVgavAgi ODisida kAraNkAkxgi nAyxyAlyada muMde hAjrupaDisalAyitu. 
\num{12} (\birx) (yAvudoV oMdu) bele utatxma sithxtiyalilx Eri: \eng{Rs.5 up on the transaction} (vAyxpArada) vahivATinalilx 5 rU.gaLaSuTx muMdAgi, 
hecAcxgi. 
\num{13} (padAthaR \mo vugaLa \vi) bele Eri: \eng{meat is up this week} I vAra mAMsada bele Eride. 
\num{14} (nATkashAleya parade) (raMgasathxLa kANisuvaMte) parade -- meVlkekx Eri, meVledudx. 
\num{15} (mAtanADuvavanu niMtiruva yA sUcisida) sathxLada yA kAldavarege baMdu, samiVpisi: \eng{the child came up and asked me the time} magu nananx baLi baMdu `eSuTx gaMTe' eMdu keVLitu. \eng{went straight up to the door} neVravAgi bAgilvarege hoVda. \eng{has been up till now} iduvarege cenAnxgi, AroVgayxvAgidAdxne. 
\num{16} \alnum{a} (hAsige \mo vugaLiMda) meVlkekxdudx. 

\alnum{b} (piVThadalilx kuLitavanu, maMDiyUri kuLitavanu) meVledudx niMtu: \eng{sprang up from his seat} avanu piVThadiMda Pakakxne meVledudx niMta. 

\alnum{c} (caTuvaTikeya sUcaneyAgi) meVledudx; meVlkekx ebibxsi
(modalAdAdxgi): \eng{put your umbrella up} ninanx Catirx bicicx meVletutx. 

\alnum{d} nililxsi; niMtiruva sithxtiyalilx: \eng{stood it up} adanunx nililxsida. 
\num{17} (\BAavayx dalilx) edudxniMtu; meVlkekx niMtu. 
\num{18} parisharxma paDedu; kalitu; shikaSxNhoMdi: \eng{he is well up in mathematics} avanige gaNitadalilx oLeLxya parisharxmavide. 
\num{19} muMduvaridu; ELigeyAgi: \eng{he is up with the leaders} avanu muMduvaridu muKMDara jte idAdxne. 
\num{20} (\nw) (cukAkxNiya \vi) gALigedurAgi. 
\num{21} daMgeyedudx. 
\num{22} (beVTe \mo vu) muMduvariyutatx; naDeyutatx. 
\num{23} (sUyaR, caMdarx, \mo vu) udayisi: \eng{the moon is up} caMdarx mUDidAdxne. 
\num{24} pUtiRyAgi yA pariNAmakAriyAgi: \eng{eat up} tiMdubiDu. \eng{drink up} kuDidubiDu. \eng{sawn up into logs} dimimxgaLAgi koyudx biTTx. 
\num{25} aDakavAda, sheVKrisida yA suBadarxvAda sithxtige taMdu: \eng{pack up} poTTxN kaTuTx. \eng{bind up} kaTuTxgaLanAnxgi mADu. \eng{store up} sheVKra mADu. \eng{lock up} surakiSxtavAgi, BadarxvAgi -- biVga hAki BadarxpaDisu. 
\num{26} meVlinadu eMdu BAvitavAda sathxLakekx yA sathxLadalilx, \kanmu\ 

\alnum{a} utatxrakekx, utatxradalilx: \eng{is up in Kashmir} utatxrada kAshimxVradalilx. 

\alnum{b} (\birx) parxmuK nagarakekx yA vishavxvidAyxnilyakekx:
\eng{went up to London} lMDanf nagarakekx hoVda. \eng{went up to
Oxford} AkfsxphaDfR vishavxvidAyxnilyakekx seVrida.  
\num{27} sidadhxpaDisida yA apeVkiSxta sithxtige: \eng{wound up the watch} gaDiyArakekx kiVlukoTTx. 
\num{28} (gaNkayaMtarxda \vi) naDeyutatx; baLakege sidadhxvAda. 
\num{29} hecucx gaTiTxyAgi yA sapxSaTxvAgi: \eng{speak up} gaTiTxyAgi yA sapxSaTxvAgi heVLu, mAtanADu. 
\num{30} mugidu hoVgi; pUtiRyAgi; sigadaMtAgi: \eng{time is up} kAl mugiduhoVyitu, hotAtxyitu; veVLe mIritu. 
\num{31} hAsigeyiMda edudx: \eng{are you up yet?} niVnu inUnx edidxdidxVyA? 
\num{32} (\kanmu\ asAdhAraNvAgi yA aniriVkiSxtavAgi) naDeyatatx; Agutatx; saMBavisutatx: \eng{something is up} EnoV Agutitxde, naDeyutitxde.}}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{be all up with} (vayxkitxge) vinAshakaravAgi; pUtiR hAnikaravAgi; Baravase, niriVkeSx illxdaMte: \eng{it is all up with him} (\AmA) (nirAsheya sUcaneyAgi) avana kathe pUreYsitu. avana kathe pUtiR mugidaMteyeV.

\num{3} \eng{up against} 

\alnum{a} hatitxravAgi; samiVpadalilx.

sikikx.

ErupeVrAgutatx.

\alnum{a} varege; tanaka: \eng{up to the present} iduvarege; ililxyatanaka. 

\alnum{b} iSuTx saMKeyxya tanaka, saMKeyxya oLage: \eng{can take up to six guests} Arakekx miVradaSuTx atithigaLanunx nAnu baramADikoLaLxbalelx.

\pron{apfhoVlfsaTxrf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} (koVNe \mo vanunx tere, jmaKAna, piVThoVpakaraNgaLu, 
\mo vugaLiMda) sajujxgoLisu.
\num{2} (kuciR \mo vakekx) metetx, baTeTxya gavasu, \mo vanunx havaNisu.
\num{3} (kuciR \mo vakekx) gavasu hAku; alMkArada baTeTx 
kavisu. }}

\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{\hyperdef{U}{upholsterpagu}{}
\eng{well-upholstered} (\hA) (vayxkitxya \vi) bojujx beLeda; ToNpanAda.}

\bentry

\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{\num{1} baLasuvudu; upayoVgisuvudu; baLake; upayoVga; parxyoVga; 
viniyoVga: \eng{put it to good use} adanunx cenAnxgi upayoVgisu. 
\eng{has passed out of use} adu Iga baLakeyalilxllx. \eng{is in daily use} 
dinabaLakeyalilxde.
\num{2} upayoVgisuva hakukx yA shakitx yA adhikAra: \eng{lost the use of 
his left arm} eDatoVLanunx baLasalu avanige sAdhayxvillx (eDatoVLanunx 
baLasuva shakitx kaLedukoMDidAdxne).
\num{3} (baLasuvudara) Pal; parxyoVjna: \eng{a blunt knife is of no use} 
moMDa cAkuviniMda yAva parxyoVjnavU illx. \eng{it is no use talking} 
mAtanADuvudariMda, mAtanADi -- parxyoVjnavillx.
\num{4} padadhxti; aBAyxsa; vADike: \eng{long use has reconciled me to it} 
diVGaRkAlda aBAyxsadiMda nAnu adanunx sarihoMdisikoMDidedxVne.
\num{5} (caciRna, ArAdhanA maMdirada) pUjA padadhxti; kamaRpadadhxti; 
dhAmiRka parxkirxyegaLu: \eng{Anglican use} iMgilxSf caciRna padadhxti.
\num{6} (\nAyxshA) (\ca) (beVrobabx PalAnuBaviya anuBoVgakAkxgi mAtarx obabxna vashadalilxruva Asitxya) PalAnuBava; anuBoVga.}}

\noindent

\dictmeaning{\num{1} \eng{have no use for} 

\alnum{a} parxyoVjnavAgadiru; agatayxvillxdiru. 

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) iSaTxvillxdiru: kaMDare Agadiru: \eng{he had no use for laggards} avanige soVmArigaLanunx kaMDare Agadu.
\num{2} \eng{make use of} baLasu; upayoVgisu; parxyoVjna paDe. 
\num{3} \eng{meant for use, not for ornament} adara udedxVsha -- baLake, 
alMkAravallx.
\num{4} \eng{use and wont} rUDhi padadhxti; sAthxpitavAda vADike.}
